newItem(key, data, int32(expiresInSeconds))\n43: \treturn s.c.Set(memcachedItem)\n44: }\n45: \n46: // GetByteArray returns the cached value as an byte array\n47: func (s *memcachedStorage) Get(ctx context.Context, key string) ([]byte, error) {\n48: \tmemcachedItem, err := s.c.Get(key)\n49: \tif errors.Is(err, memcache.ErrCacheMiss) {\n50: \t\treturn nil, ErrCacheItemNotFound\n51: \t}\n52: \n53: \tif err != nil {\n54: \t\treturn nil, err\n55: \t}\n56: \n57: \treturn memcachedItem.Value, nil\n58: }\n59: \n60: // Delete delete a key from the cache\n61: func (s *memcachedStorage) Delete(ctx result caching layer is implemented across multiple Go packages with a clear abstraction hierarchy:\\n\\n## Cache Service Interface & Implementation (pkg/services/caching/)\\n\\nThe core caching service is defined in pkg/services/caching/service.go with the CachingService interface that has two main methods: HandleQueryRequest() and HandleResourceRequest(). The OSSCachingService in the same file provides a no-op implementation for the open-source version. The CachingServiceClient wrapper (pkg/services/caching/service.go) provides the WithQueryDataCaching() and WithCallResourceCaching() methods that wrap query execution with caching logic.\\n\\n## Cache Key Generation (pkg/services/caching/service.go)\\n\\nQuery cache keys are generated using the GetKey() function which uses JSONEncoder to serialize query parameters and SHA256KeyFunc to create a SHA256 hash of the serialized query. This generates deterministic keys like \\\"namespace:prefix:sha256hash\\\" that allow cache hits for identical queries.\\n\\n## Cache Storage Backends (pkg/infra/remotecache/)\\n\\nThree cache backend implementations are available:\\n\\n1. **Redis Backend** (pkg/infra/remotecache/redis_storage.go): Uses the redis/go-redis v9 client with configurable connection strings supporting TLS, authentication, and connection pooling. Implements Get(), Set(), and Delete() operations with configurable TTL.\\n\\n2. **Memcached Backend** (pkg/infra/remotecache/memcached_storage.go): Uses bradfitz/gomemcache client. Implements the same CacheStorage interface for Get(), Set(), Delete() operations.\\n\\n3. **Database Backend** (pkg/infra/remotecache/database_storage.go): Stores cache in the database using the cache_data table. Includes garbage collection via a 10-minute background job (Run() method) that deletes expired cache entries. Uses UPSERT pattern (INSERT with UPDATE fallback) to handle concurrent updates.\\n\\nThe RemoteCache class (pkg/infra/remotecache/remotecache.go) abstracts these backends and provides optional encryption wrapper (encryptedCacheStorage) and key prefix wrapper (prefixCacheStorage) for composable cache behavior.\\n\\n## Cache TTL Policy (Dashboard Panels)\\n\\nQuery caching TTL is configured at the panel level through the QueryCachingTTL field defined in:\\n- pkg/kinds/dashboard/dashboard_spec_gen.go\\n- apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/v2beta1/dashboard_spec_gen.go\\n- apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/v2alpha1/dashboard_spec_gen.go\\n\\nThe migration conversion files (apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/conversion/) handle backward compatibility when converting between dashboard schema versions (v1beta1, v2alpha1, v2beta1).\\n\\n## Cache Invalidation on Dashboard Save\\n\\nDashboard save events trigger cache invalidation through the DashboardActivityChannel interface. The implementation is in:\\n- pkg/services/live/features/dashboard.go: DashboardHandler.DashboardSaved() broadcasts a dashboardEvent with ActionSaved when a dashboard is saved\\n- pkg/services/live/live.go: CoreGrafanaScope.Dashboards field holds the DashboardActivityChannel\\n\\nThe DashboardSaved() event can be used by cache implementations to invalidate cached query results for panels in that dashboard.\\n\\n## Cache Middleware Integration (pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/caching_middleware.go)\\n\\nThe CachingMiddleware intercepts QueryData requests and calls CachingServiceClient.WithQueryDataCaching() to check the cache before executing queries and cache results afterward. This is integrated into the plugin handler chain via NewCachingMiddleware().\\n\\n## Datasource Caching Configuration (pkg/plugins/models.go)\\n\\nDataSources have a QueryCachingConfig struct with Enabled bool and TTLMs (TTL in milliseconds) fields that are populated by Enterprise hooks.\\n\\n## Public Dashboard Query Caching (pkg/services/publicdashboards/)\\n\\nPublic dashboards use QueryCachingTTL settings (pkg/services/publicdashboards/models/models.go) that are passed to queries via QueryCachingTTL field in the PublicDashboardQueryDTO. The service layer (pkg/services/publicdashboards/service/query.go) sets this value on queries when executing public dashboard queries.\\n\\n## Cache Metrics (pkg/services/caching/metrics.go)\\n\\nThree Prometheus histograms track cache performance:\\n- QueryCachingRequestHistogram: request duration by datasource_type, cache status (HIT/MISS/BYPASS/ERROR/DISABLED), and query_type\\n- ShouldCacheQueryHistogram: duration of cache decision logic\\n- ResourceCachingRequestHistogram: resource request caching by plugin_id and cache status\\n\\n## Cache Configuration (pkg/setting/setting_remote_cache.go)\\n\\nRemote cache is configured via the [remote_cache] section with Name (redis/memcached/database), ConnStr (connection string), Prefix (key prefix), and Encryption (enable encryption) options.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":5,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1613,"cache_read_input_tokens":104354,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1613},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ba1f4bb4-60b0-4372-9782-df885daacbbc","uuid":"ebe3556e-688e-492f-8678-b56c29ce96c8"}

result caching layer is implemented across multiple Go packages with a clear abstraction hierarchy:\\n\\n## Cache Service Interface & Implementation (pkg/services/caching/)\\n\\nThe core caching service is defined in pkg/services/caching/service.go with the CachingService interface that has two main methods: HandleQueryRequest() and HandleResourceRequest(). The OSSCachingService in the same file provides a no-op implementation for the open-source version. The CachingServiceClient wrapper (pkg/services/caching/service.go) provides the WithQueryDataCaching() and WithCallResourceCaching() methods that wrap query execution with caching logic.\\n\\n## Cache Key Generation (pkg/services/caching/service.go)\\n\\nQuery cache keys are generated using the GetKey() function which uses JSONEncoder to serialize query parameters and SHA256KeyFunc to create a SHA256 hash of the serialized query. This generates deterministic keys like \\\"namespace:prefix:sha256hash\\\" that allow cache hits for identical queries.\\n\\n## Cache Storage Backends (pkg/infra/remotecache/)\\n\\nThree cache backend implementations are available:\\n\\n1. **Redis Backend** (pkg/infra/remotecache/redis_storage.go): Uses the redis/go-redis v9 client with configurable connection strings supporting TLS, authentication, and connection pooling. Implements Get(), Set(), and Delete() operations with configurable TTL.\\n\\n2. **Memcached Backend** (pkg/infra/remotecache/memcached_storage.go): Uses bradfitz/gomemcache client. Implements the same CacheStorage interface for Get(), Set(), Delete() operations.\\n\\n3. **Database Backend** (pkg/infra/remotecache/database_storage.go): Stores cache in the database using the cache_data table. Includes garbage collection via a 10-minute background job (Run() method) that deletes expired cache entries. Uses UPSERT pattern (INSERT with UPDATE fallback) to handle concurrent updates.\\n\\nThe RemoteCache class (pkg/infra/remotecache/remotecache.go) abstracts these backends and provides optional encryption wrapper (encryptedCacheStorage) and key prefix wrapper (prefixCacheStorage) for composable cache behavior.\\n\\n## Cache TTL Policy (Dashboard Panels)\\n\\nQuery caching TTL is configured at the panel level through the QueryCachingTTL field defined in:\\n- pkg/kinds/dashboard/dashboard_spec_gen.go\\n- apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/v2beta1/dashboard_spec_gen.go\\n- apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/v2alpha1/dashboard_spec_gen.go\\n\\nThe migration conversion files (apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/conversion/) handle backward compatibility when converting between dashboard schema versions (v1beta1, v2alpha1, v2beta1).\\n\\n## Cache Invalidation on Dashboard Save\\n\\nDashboard save events trigger cache invalidation through the DashboardActivityChannel interface. The implementation is in:\\n- pkg/services/live/features/dashboard.go: DashboardHandler.DashboardSaved() broadcasts a dashboardEvent with ActionSaved when a dashboard is saved\\n- pkg/services/live/live.go: CoreGrafanaScope.Dashboards field holds the DashboardActivityChannel\\n\\nThe DashboardSaved() event can be used by cache implementations to invalidate cached query results for panels in that dashboard.\\n\\n## Cache Middleware Integration (pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/caching_middleware.go)\\n\\nThe CachingMiddleware intercepts QueryData requests and calls CachingServiceClient.WithQueryDataCaching() to check the cache before executing queries and cache results afterward. This is integrated into the plugin handler chain via NewCachingMiddleware().\\n\\n## Datasource Caching Configuration (pkg/plugins/models.go)\\n\\nDataSources have a QueryCachingConfig struct with Enabled bool and TTLMs (TTL in milliseconds) fields that are populated by Enterprise hooks.\\n\\n## Public Dashboard Query Caching (pkg/services/publicdashboards/)\\n\\nPublic dashboards use QueryCachingTTL settings (pkg/services/publicdashboards/models/models.go) that are passed to queries via QueryCachingTTL field in the PublicDashboardQueryDTO. The service layer (pkg/services/publicdashboards/service/query.go) sets this value on queries when executing public dashboard queries.\\n\\n## Cache Metrics (pkg/services/caching/metrics.go)\\n\\nThree Prometheus histograms track cache performance:\\n- QueryCachingRequestHistogram: request duration by datasource_type, cache status (HIT/MISS/BYPASS/ERROR/DISABLED), and query_type\\n- ShouldCacheQueryHistogram: duration of cache decision logic\\n- ResourceCachingRequestHistogram: resource request caching by plugin_id and cache status\\n\\n## Cache Configuration (pkg/setting/setting_remote_cache.go)\\n\\nRemote cache is configured via the [remote_cache] section with Name (redis/memcached/database), ConnStr (connection string), Prefix (key prefix), and Encryption (enable encryption) options.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
